**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bgc5z86utjwh/android/app/src/main/java/com/github/manager/MainActivity.kt]
Thought: 
Command: create
Created File with Text:
```
package com.github.manager

import android.annotation.SuppressLint
import android.graphics.Color
import android.os.Bundle
import android.view.View
import android.view.WindowManager
import android.webkit.WebResourceRequest
import android.webkit.WebSettings
import android.webkit.WebView
import android.webkit.WebViewClient
import androidx.appcompat.app.AppCompatActivity
import androidx.core.view.WindowCompat
import androidx.core.view.WindowInsetsControllerCompat

class MainActivity : AppCompatActivity() {

    private lateinit var webView: WebView

    @SuppressLint("SetJavaScriptEnabled")
    override fun onCreate(savedInstanceState: Bundle?) {
        super.onCreate(savedInstanceState)

        // 全屏沉浸式——让 WebView 延伸到状态栏 / 导航栏下方
        WindowCompat.setDecorFitsSystemWindows(window, false)
        window.statusBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        window.navigationBarColor = Color.TRANSPARENT
        WindowInsetsControllerCompat(window, window.decorView).apply {
            isAppearanceLightStatusBars = false
            isAppearanceLightNavigationBars = false
        }

        setContentView(R.layout.activity_main)

        webView = findViewById(R.id.webView)

        webView.settings.apply {
            javaScriptEnabled = true
            domStorageEnabled = true          // localStorage / sessionStorage
            databaseEnabled = true
            allowFileAccess = true            // 读取 assets 内的 index.html
            allowContentAccess = true
            // 允许 file:// 页面访问 https:// (GitHub API)
            mixedContentMode = WebSettings.MIXED_CONTENT_ALWAYS_ALLOW
            cacheMode = WebSettings.LOAD_DEFAULT
            // 视口自适应
            useWideViewPort = true
            loadWithOverviewMode = true
            // 禁用内置缩放控件，由 Web 端 viewport meta 控制
            setSupportZoom(false)
            displayZoomControls = false
            builtInZoomControls = false
            // 媒体自动播放
            mediaPlaybackRequiresUserGesture = false
        }

        webView.setBackgroundColor(Color.TRANSPARENT)

        webView.webViewClient = object : WebViewClient() {
            override fun shouldOverrideUrlLoading(
                view: WebView?,
                request: WebResourceRequest?,
            ): Boolean {
                val url = request?.url?.toString() ?: return false
                // file:// 和 https:// 均在 WebView 内处理（GitHub API + OAuth Device Flow）
                if (url.startsWith("file://") ||
                    url.startsWith("https://") ||
                    url.startsWith("http://")
                ) return false
                return true
            }

            override fun onPageFinished(view: WebView?, url: String?) {
                super.onPageFinished(view, url)
                // 页面加载完成后隐藏背景防止白屏闪烁
                webView.visibility = View.VISIBLE
            }
        }

        // 屏幕旋转等配置变化时恢复页面状态，避免重新加载
        if (savedInstanceState != null) {
            webView.restoreState(savedInstanceState)
        } else {
            webView.visibility = View.INVISIBLE // 加载前隐藏，onPageFinished 后显示
            webView.loadUrl("file:///android_asset/index.html")
        }
    }

    override fun onSaveInstanceState(outState: Bundle) {
        super.onSaveInstanceState(outState)
        webView.saveState(outState)
    }

    @Deprecated("onBackPressed is deprecated but still needed for WebView navigation")
    override fun onBackPressed() {
        if (webView.canGoBack()) {
            webView.goBack()
        } else {
            @Suppress("DEPRECATION")
            super.onBackPressed()
        }
    }
}

```

**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-bgc5z86utjwh/.github/workflows/deploy.yml]
Thought: 现在更新 GitHub Actions workflow，拆分为三个 Job：
Command: str_replace
Old String: ```
# GitHub Pages 自动部署工作流
# 推送到 main 分支时自动构建并发布到 GitHub Pages，同时生成可内嵌 APK 的 dist.zip
name: Deploy to GitHub Pages

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  workflow_dispatch: # 支持手动触发

# 设置 GITHUB_TOKEN 权限以允许部署到 GitHub Pages
permissions:
  contents: read
  pages: write
  id-token: write

# 只允许一个并发部署，新部署会取消正在进行的部署
concurrency:
  group: pages
  cancel-in-progress: true

jobs:
  build-and-deploy:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: 检出代码
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: 安装 pnpm
        uses: pnpm/action-setup@v4
        with:
          version: 9
          # pnpm/action-setup 自身会缓存 store；
          # 不在 setup-node 中再配 cache: pnpm，
          # 避免 lockfile 不存在时报 "Dependencies lock file is not found"

      - name: 设置 Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20
          # cache: pnpm  ← 已移除；lockfile 首次提交前不存在会导致此步骤失败

      - name: 安装依赖
        # --frozen-lockfile 确保 CI 使用锁定版本，不意外升级依赖
        run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: 构建
        # package.json 的 build 脚本仅用于本地 lint，
        # CI 中直接调用 vite build 避免被 echo 跳过
        run: pnpm exec vite build

      # ── APK 内嵌产物 ──────────────────────────────────────────
      # 将 dist/ 压缩为 dist.zip，可直接复制到 Android assets/ 目录
      # 在 WebView 中通过 file:///android_asset/index.html 加载
      - name: 打包 WebView APK 可用 dist.zip
        run: cd dist && zip -r ../dist.zip . && cd ..

      - name: 上传 dist.zip 为 Actions Artifact
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: webview-apk-dist
          path: dist.zip
          retention-days: 30
      # ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

      - name: 配置 GitHub Pages
        uses: actions/configure-pages@v5

      - name: 上传构建产物
        uses: actions/upload-pages-artifact@v3
        with:
          path: dist

      - name: 部署到 GitHub Pages
        id: deployment
        uses: actions/deploy-pages@v4
```
New String: ```
# GitHub Pages 自动部署 + Android APK 构建工作流
# 推送到 main 分支时：
#   1. 构建 Web 应用（dist/）
#   2. 部署到 GitHub Pages
#   3. 打包 Android APK（WebView 壳 + dist/ 资源）
name: Deploy & Build APK

on:
  push:
    branches: [main]
  workflow_dispatch: # 支持手动触发

# GITHUB_TOKEN 权限：Pages 部署需要 pages + id-token
permissions:
  contents: read
  pages: write
  id-token: write

# 同组并发：新部署取消旧部署（仅影响 Pages，APK 构建不受影响）
concurrency:
  group: pages
  cancel-in-progress: true

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
jobs:

  # ── Job 1：构建 Web 应用 ───────────────────────────────────────
  build-web:
    name: 构建 Web 应用
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: 检出代码
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: 安装 pnpm
        uses: pnpm/action-setup@v4
        with:
          version: 9
          # pnpm/action-setup 自身处理 store 缓存；
          # 不在 setup-node 中配 cache: pnpm，
          # 避免首次提交时 lockfile 不存在导致步骤失败

      - name: 设置 Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 20

      - name: 安装依赖
        run: pnpm install --frozen-lockfile

      - name: 构建 Web 应用
        run: pnpm exec vite build

      - name: 上传 Web 构建产物（供后续 Job 使用）
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: web-dist
          path: dist
          retention-days: 1   # 仅在本次 workflow 期间保留

      - name: 配置 GitHub Pages
        uses: actions/configure-pages@v5

      - name: 上传 Pages 产物
        uses: actions/upload-pages-artifact@v3
        with:
          path: dist

  # ── Job 2：部署到 GitHub Pages ─────────────────────────────────
  deploy-pages:
    name: 部署到 GitHub Pages
    needs: build-web
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment:
      name: github-pages
      url: ${{ steps.deployment.outputs.page_url }}
    steps:
      - name: 部署到 GitHub Pages
        id: deployment
        uses: actions/deploy-pages@v4

  # ── Job 3：构建 Android APK ────────────────────────────────────
  build-apk:
    name: 构建 Android APK
    needs: build-web
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: 检出代码（含 android/ 项目源码）
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: 下载 Web 构建产物
        uses: actions/download-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: web-dist
          path: dist

      - name: 将 Web 资源复制到 Android assets
        run: |
          mkdir -p android/app/src/main/assets
          cp -r dist/. android/app/src/main/assets/

      - name: 设置 JDK 17
        uses: actions/setup-java@v4
        with:
          java-version: '17'
          distribution: 'temurin'

      - name: 设置 Gradle 8.7
        uses: gradle/actions/setup-gradle@v3
        with:
          gradle-version: '8.7'
          # 缓存 Gradle 依赖，加快后续构建
          cache-read-only: false

      - name: 生成 local.properties（指向预装 Android SDK）
        run: echo "sdk.dir=$ANDROID_HOME" > android/local.properties

      - name: 接受 Android SDK 许可证
        run: |
          yes | $ANDROID_HOME/cmdline-tools/latest/bin/sdkmanager --licenses 2>/dev/null || true

      - name: 构建 Debug APK
        working-directory: android
        run: gradle assembleDebug --no-daemon

      - name: 上传 APK 产物
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: github-manager-apk
          path: android/app/build/outputs/apk/debug/app-debug.apk
          retention-days: 30

```

</action>
